     <!-- Finance specific Quote Search bar. Includes Quote Search form at left side and the Market Time(status) at right side. -->
     <div class="yom-bar">
      <div class="yog-grid yog-24u">
       <div class="yog-wrap">
        <div class="yog-col yog-12u">
         <div class="yog-wrap">
          <div class="yog-col yog-6u">
           <div class="yom-mod ticker-search" id="searchQuotes" mode="search">
            <div class="bd">
             <form action="/q" class="get-quotes" id="quote" name="quote">
              <label for="txtQuotes">
               Search for share prices
              </label>
              <input autocomplete="off" class="get-quotes-box" id="txtQuotes" name="s" placeholder="Enter Symbol" type="text" value=""/>
              <input autocomplete="off" id="get_quote_logic_opt" name="ql" type="hidden" value="1"/>
              <input class="get-quotes-button rapid-nf" id="btnQuotes" type="submit" value="Look Up"/>
             </form>
             <script>
              YUI().use('node', 'event', function (Y) {
						var tempInputElem = document.createElement('input');
					    var isPlaceHolder = ('placeholder' in tempInputElem);
		                if (!isPlaceHolder) {
		                	var acInputBoxEl = Y.one("#txtQuotes");
		                    var placeHolderValue = acInputBoxEl.getAttribute('placeholder');
		                    var preInitVal = acInputBoxEl.get('value');
		                    acInputBoxEl.on("focus", function() {
		                        acInputBoxEl.set('value', '');
		                        acInputBoxEl.removeClass("hint");
		                    });
		                    acInputBoxEl.on("blur", function() {
		                        var value = acInputBoxEl.get('value');
		                        if (value === null || value.length === 0) {
		                            acInputBoxEl.set('value', placeHolderValue);
		                            acInputBoxEl.addClass("hint");
		                        }

		                    });

		                    if (preInitVal === undefined || preInitVal.length === 0 || preInitVal === placeHolderValue) {
		                        acInputBoxEl.set('value', placeHolderValue);
		                        acInputBoxEl.addClass("hint");
		                    }
		                }
					});
             </script>
             <div class="yui-ac-container yui3-aclist" id="quoteContainer" style="display:none">
              <div class="yui-ac-content yui3-aclist-content">
               <div class="yui-ac-hd" style="display: none;">
               </div>
               <div class="yui-ac-bd">
                <ul id="resQuotes">
                </ul>
               </div>
               <div class="yui-ac-ft">
                <div class="moreresults">
                 <a href="javascript:;">
                 </a>
                </div>

                 <em>
                  Tip :
                 </em>
                 Use comma (,) to separate multiple quotes.
                 <a href="http://help.yahoo.com/l/ca/yahoo/finance/quotes/quotelookup.html">
                  Learn more...
                 </a>
                </div>
               </div>

              yfs_common_params = { "market" : {"NAME" : "",
                              "ID" : "CA",
                              "TZ" : "",
                              "TZOFFSET" : "-18000",
                              "open" : "",
                              "close" : "",

        <div class="yom-mod yom-art-hd" id="mediaarticlehead">
         <div class="bd">
          <h1 class="headline">
           Royal LePage agent Dagmara Lulek charging $50 to view Toronto Beach home
          </h1>
          <cite class="byline vcard">
           By
           <span class="fn">
            <a href="/blogs/author/jennifer-kwan-/" rel="author">
             Jennifer Kwan
            </a>
           </span>
           |
           <span class="provider org">
            <a href="/blogs/pay-day-/">
             Pay Day
            </a>
           </span>
           
           <abbr title="2013-05-07T17:52:14Z">
            Tue, 7 May, 2013 1:52 PM EDT
           </abbr>
          </cite>
         </div>
        </div>
        <div class="yom-remote">
         <div class="yom-loading" id="mediasocialbuttonseasy_container">
          <!-- -->
         </div>
        </div>
        <div class="yom-mod yom-art-related yom-art-lead" id="mediaarticlelead">
         <div class="bd">
          <ul>
           <li class="photo first last">
            <a class="media rapid-nf" data-ylk="pkg:78a57af5-a860-47ef-9f54-a8c8d7f9c8fb;ver:bf485bc9-b73b-11e2-9ede-49c2fe039e6c;ct:p;" href="/photos/toronto-beach-home-photo--2146767217.html">
             <div class="yom-art-lead-img">
              <img alt="The $4.99-million waterfront Toronto home is shown in a handout photo courtesy of Royal LePage." height="420" src="https://s1.yimg.com/bt/api/res/1.2/Nt9TyOyPSCFyJ_yp827t1g--/YXBwaWQ9eW5ld3M7Y2g9NDgwO2NyPTE7Y3c9NzIwO2R4PTA7ZHk9MDtmaT11bGNyb3A7aD00MjA7aWw9cGxhbmU7cT03NTt3PTYzMA--/http://l.yimg.com/os/publish-images/finance/2013-05-07/bbd0f3d8-06bd-4ce3-9974-5fe4478e64a5_Front.jpg" title="The $4.99-million waterfront Toronto home is shown in a handout photo courtesy of Royal LePage." width="630"/>
             </div>
            </a>
            <p>
             Yahoo Finance Canada/Royal LePage - The $4.99-million waterfront Toronto home is shown in a handout photo courtesy of Royal LePage.
            </p>
           </li>
          </ul>
         </div>
        </div>
        <div itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Article">
         <meta content="2013-05-07T17:52:14Z" itemprop="datePublished"/>
         <meta content="Pay Day" itemprop="provider"/>
         <meta content="Royal LePage agent Dagmara Lulek charging $50 to view Toronto Beach home" itemprop="headline"/>
         <meta content="Jennifer Kwan" itemprop="author"/>
         <meta content="The listing says it all: it's an exceptionally rare and highly-coveted Toronto Beach-area home with direct waterfront access on an acre of land. Theres a two-floor guest house and a wrap-around porch and much, much more. Just as rare is  Continue reading " itemprop="description"/>
         <div class="yom-mod yom-art-content " id="mediablogbody" itemprop="articleBody">
          <div class="bd">
           <!-- google_ad_section_start -->
           <p class="first">
            <a href="http://www-d.royallepage.ca/en-ca/ontario/toronto/property/MLSE2606392/884833/1-fallingbrook-rd#.UYk5Y8r5fHS">
             The listing says it all
            </a>
            : At almost $5 million, it's an exceptionally rare and highly-coveted Toronto Beach-area home with direct waterfront access on an acre of land. There's a two-floor guest house and a wrap-around porch and much, much more.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            Just as rare is the section that reads, "$50 Charitable Donation Required/Accepted Prior To Showing Payable To SickKids Foundation. Receipt Will Be Provided."
            <br/>
            <br/>
            The idea is to keep the gawkers away, said Dagmara Lulek, the Royal LePage listing agent, who along with Vito Doria proposed the idea to the owner.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            Since the owner prefers a non-traditional viewing of the house, agents and their interested clients have been asked to make donations to browse the property at 1 Fallingbrook Rd. The money will go to SickKids, a not-for-profit children's charity.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            "This is somebody's home. We can't have people coming through the home just to be curious," says Lulek.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            "That's not what it's about. It's about people that are in the market and people who want to see the house because they're interested in buying it."
            <br/>
            <br/>
            The unusual move has raised some eyebrows from realtors, says Lulek, but potential buyers have applauded the move: they can understand why an owner wants to keep people from unnecessarily traipsing through their house. In the end, it's a marketing technique that benefits everyone, she adds.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            The Real Estate Council of Ontario sees nothing wrong with the tactic, provided the donation requirement isnt false, misleading or deceptive and its being done with the sellers support, a spokesperson said.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            The house dates back to the early 1900s and can only be renovated because it has been designated a heritage property, says Lulek.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            A key selling feature of the estate is the layout, which includes three separate units on one property, along with its proximity to the water.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            But that comes with a price tag of $4.99 million. The taxes alone are roughly $25,000 a year.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            The $50-a-glimpse was first spotted by the
            <a href="http://www.thestar.com/business/real_estate/2013/05/07/beach_home_for_sale_but_itll_cost_you_50_just_to_see_it.html">
             Toronto Star newspaper
            </a>
            . There are no pictures of the interior on the Multiple Listing Service (MLS), and according to the newspaper the owner claimed she was pulling the house off the market when the reporter requested a tour.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            "A few grace a glossy marketing brochure and show a main house that looks less grand than a lot like Grandmas. The kitchen may lack a Wolf range or a Sub Zero Fridge, but it does boast two dishwashers," the paper notes.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            "The wow factor is in the spacious living and dining room with French doors and oversized windows looking out over the lake."
           </p>
           <!-- google_ad_section_end -->
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>

	        window.addEventListener("message", sendMessage, false);

	        window.attachEvent("onmessage", sendMessage);
